### Tool call: browser_evaluate
- Args
```json
{
  "function": "() => { var feed = document.querySelectorAll('iframe'); var texts = []; for (var i = 0; i < feed.length; i++) { try { texts.push('iframe ' + i + ': ' + feed[i].src.substring(0, 80)); } catch(e) {} } var posts = document.querySelectorAll('[class*=\"feed\"] p, .content'); var result = []; for (var j = 0; j < Math.min(posts.length, 5); j++) { result.push(posts[j].textContent.substring(0, 60)); } return { iframes: texts.slice(0, 5), samplePosts: result }; }"
}
```

